Town Board Regular Meeting Minutes 
Tuesday, March 4, 2025 – 2:00 PM 
 
 
I. Call to Order 
The meeting was called to order at 2:02 PM by Supervisor Tim Hubbard 
 
Attendee Name Title Status Arrived 
Tim Hubbard Supervisor Absent  
Kenneth Rothwell Councilman Present  
Robert Kern Councilman Present  
Denise Merrifield Councilwoman Present  
Joann Waski Councilwoman Present  
II. Notice 
1. Notice with Zoom Credentials  
 
III. Invocation - Reverend David Cooke - Calvary Baptist Church of Riverhead 
IV. Announcements 
V. Correspondence 
1. Letter from Lorraine Wilson - Reeves Park Parking Lot  
 
VI. Reports 
VII. Public Hearings 
  - 2:00 PM Public Hearing Chapter 301-254 Article XLVIII Signs  
Greg Bergman from planning gave overview of amendment. No public 
comments, held open for written comments till March 14, at 4:30 PM 
 
  - 2:00 PM Public Hearing Chapter 301-305 Article LVI Site Plan Review  
Greg Bergman gave overview of amendment to include an additional 6 month 
extension of preliminary site plans. Martin Sendlewski via Zoom commented 
and questioned the need for any time constraints. Held open for written 
comments till March 24, at 4:30 PM 
  
For more information visit our website at www.townofriverheadny.gov  
 
 
  - 2:00 PM Public Hearing Chapter 301-197 Article XLI Pine Barrens Overlay  
Matthew Charters from Planning gave overview of amendments to Chapter 
301, to include all hearings concerning Art.XLVIII, Art LIID, Art.LII and Art LI, 
All amendments are being considered to adhere to the current updated 
master plan recently adopted. No public comment. Held open for written 
comment till March 14, at 4:30PM 
 
  - 2:00 PM Public Hearing Chapter 301 Article XLVIII Signs  
 
  - 2:00 PM Public Hearing Chapter 301-274 Part 3, Article LI Wireless 
Communication  
 
  - 2:00 PM Public Hearing Chapter 301-281 Commercial Solar Energy 
Production Systems  
 
  - 2:00 PM Public Hearing Chapter 301-283.31 Article LIID Battery Energy 
Storage  
 
  - 2:10 PM Public Hearing Chapter 229-9 Excavation and Grading Fees  
Meeting opened at 2:22 PM, Erik Howard Town Atty gave overview of the 
amendment to include a rate increase of $1.00 per yard of excavated export 
of material, or import of material for grading or excavation. No public 
comment, Held open for written comment till March 14, at 4:30 PM . 
 
VIII. Comments on Resolutions 
Cindy Clifford spoke on resolution 230 concerning new rules and procedures for 
Town Board meetings, and the restrictions they may cause for residents, also spoke 
against approval of Negative Declaration awarded to Island Water Park (Reso 234). 
John McAuliff spoke on resolution 230, and alluded to the Republican town board 
doing this to silence Democrats, and only Riverhead residents should have the 
ability to speak at Town Board meetings. 
Claudette Bianco spoke against resolution 234 awarding a neg declaration for Island 
Water Park 
Barbara Blass spoke on Resolution 234, stating SEQRA processes, and reasons 
why the Town should not award a negative declaration. 
Kevin Shea (Via Zoom) spoke about resolution 230, and read prepared notes as to 
why it is restrictive and remedies to allow a better standard.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
NOTICE REGARDING TOWN BOARD MEETING 
PLEASE TAKE NOTICE that the Town Board Meeting scheduled for March 4, 2025 at 2:00 p.m. at 
Riverhead Town Hall, 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York will proceed as scheduled.     
PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE , that in addition to in person atte ndance, the public can 
view the March 4, 2025 meeting of the Town Board via the following methods:  
1. Live stream; namely, by viewing it on your television on Channel 22;  
2. Logging on the Town of Riverhead website, www.townofriverheadny.gov and clicking 
on the link “Channel 22” on Quick Links on the home page or by connecting to the URL, 
which is as follows: townofriverheadny.viebit.com/player_live.php  
3.  Zoom Meeting, log in as follows: 
https://us02web.zoom.us/j/87199120378?pwd=2QTkwK54i9ktgP2mKHtfuK2Fdsd2Tx.1 
 
Webinar ID:  871 9912 0378      Password:  191173       Dial by your location: (929) 205-6099 
PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE that the public hearings subject to participation via Zoom 
are as follows: 
1) 2:00 Public Hearing to consider a Local Law to Amend Chapter 301 Zoning and Land 
Development, Part 3 Supplementary Use Regulations, Article XLVIII Signs, §301-254 H. 
Zoning Use Districts. The intent of the proposed legislation is to implement recommendations 
of the 2024 Comprehensive Plan Update to remove Industrial A, B, and C and include 
Calverton Industrial and Light Industrial; 
 
2) 2:00 Public Hearing to consider a proposed local law amending Chapter 301 of the 
Riverhead Town Code entitled, CHAPTER 301 OF THE RIVERHEAD TOWN CODE 
ENTITLED “ZONING AND LAND DEVELOPMENT, ARTICLE XLVIII: SIGNS”; 
 
3) 2:00 Public Hearing to consider a proposed local law amending Chapter 301 of the 
Riverhead Town Code entitled, CHAPTER 301 OF THE RIVERHEAD TOWN CODE 
ENTITLED “ZONING AND LAND DEVELOPMENT, ARTICLE LVI: SITE PLAN REVIEW”; 
 
4) 2:00 Public Hearing to consider a Local Law to Amend Chapter 301 Zoning and Land 
Development, Part 2 Districts, Article XLI Pine Barrens Overlay District, §301-197 A. (8) (a) 
Clearing and Open Space Standards. The intent of the proposed legislation is to implement 
recommendations of the 2024 Comprehensive Plan Update to remove Industrial A, B, and C 
and include Calverton Industrial and Light Industrial. 
 
5) 2:00 Public Hearing to consider a Local Law to Amend Chapter 301 Zoning and Land 
Development, Part 3 Supplementary Use Regulations, Article LI Wireless Communications 
Tower, Antennas, and Satellite Earth Stations, §301-274 Permit Requirement; Applicability. 
The intent of the proposed legislation is to implement recommendations of the 2024 
Comprehensive Plan Update to remove Industrial A and Industrial C and include Calverton 
Industrial and Light Industrial. 
 
6) 2:00 Public Hearing to consider a Local Law to Amend Chapter 301 Zoning and Land 
Development, Part 3 Supplementary Use Regulations, Article LII Commercial Solar Energy 
Production Systems, §301-281 B. & C. Purposes; permitted districts; definitions. The intent of 
the proposed legislation is to implement recommendations of the 2024 Comprehensive Plan

PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE, that upon entering the Zoom meeting, you will be 
placed in a virtual audience. From there, you may either passively watch the public hearing 
live, or communicate to the moderator/host your request to make a comment during the 
public comment section for PUBLIC HEARINGS, RESOLUTIONS and/or OPEN 
COMMENTS. To alert the moderator/host of your desire to be heard, use the “CHAT” or 
“RAISE HAND” feature, then use the “CHAT” feature to inform the moderator/host of the 
following: 
1) Name; 2) Hamlet; 3) Public Hearing, Resolution and/or Open Comment Topic. 
 
If you are calling in, please dial *9 to “raise your hand”, so we can acknowledge your request 
to speak. 
 
When it is your turn to speak, your status will be temporarily changed so you can be unmuted 
and visible for the five-minute comment period. After five minutes, you will be placed back in 
the audience. 
 
Comments/questions will be limited to five minutes. Please be patient; your admittance will be 
based on the volume of participants. Any problems or issues getting to the Town Board meeting 
via telephone or computer should be directed to (631) 727-3200 x655.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
PUBLIC NOTICE 
 
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE, that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board 
of the Town of Riverhead, at 4 West Second Street , Riverhead, New York at its regular 
meeting held on March 4, 2025 at 2:00 p.m. to consider a Local Law to Amend Chapter 301 
Zoning and Land Development, Part 3 Supplementary Use Regulations, Article XLVIII Signs, 
§301-254 H. Zoning Use Districts. The intent of the proposed legislation is to implement 
recommendations of the 2024 Comprehensive Plan Update to remove Industrial A, B, and C 
and include Calverton Industrial and Light Industrial. 
 A copy of the entire text of the adopted local law and the provisions of the existing 
law to be amended may be reviewed at the Office of the Town Clerk, 4 W Second Street, 
Riverhead, New York 11901, between the hours of 8:30 a.m. and 4:30 p.m., Monday 
through Friday and can be accessed on the Town of Riverhead website at: 
www.townofriverheadny.gov under the Agenda and Minutes for the February 19, 2025  
Town Board Meeting.  
Dated:  Riverhead, New York 
   February 19, 2025  
 
 
BY ORDER OF THE TOWN BOARD 
OF THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
JAMES M. WOOTEN, TOWN CLERK 
 
7.1.a
Packet Pg. 25
Attachment: Reso#195-Public Notice to Amend Chapter 301 Part 3 Article XLVIII Signs Chapter 301-254 Zoning Use Districts  (2025-8 : 2:00 PM
 
 
§ 301-254. Zoning use district regulations. 
H. Ind A, Ind B CI, and LI. In the Industrial A (Ind A), Industrial B (Ind B) Calverton Industrial 
(CI) and Industrial C (Ind C)  Light Industrial (LI) Zoning Use Districts, all signs are 
permitted, with the exception of: 
(1) Internally illuminated (including neon) signs, except in windows. 
(2) Electronic time/temperature display. 
(3) Roof signs (except on mansard roof(s). 
 
 
 
 
 
Underlines represent additions 
Strikethrough represents deletions

§ 301-305 § 301-305

§ 301-305. Application procedure; fees. [Amended 12-2-2003 by L.L. No. 26-2003; 
4-19-2005 by L.L. No. 10-2005; 4-19-2005 by L.L. No. 11-2005; 11-21-2006 by L.L. No. 
48-2006; 11-7-2007 by L.L. No. 33-2007; 12-6-2011 by L.L. No. 24-2011] 
B. Preliminary site plan application. 
(7) Decision on preliminary site plan application. 
(c) Upon written request by the applicant and prior to the expiration set forth in 
§ 301-305B(7)(b) above, the preliminary site plan approval may be extended for 
an additional six -month period of time after due consideration by the reviewing 
board. No more than two (2) six -month extensions shall be granted by the 
reviewing board .  If an ap plicant fails to apply for final site plan review and 
approval within one year of preliminary site plan approval or, to the extent granted 
by the reviewing board,  within the two (2) six-month extension period(s), the 
Planning Department shall deem the site plan application abandoned such that no 
further action shall be taken by the Planning Department and/or  any such other 
board vested with authority to  review, approve or deny a site plan application, 
and, in such event that an application is abandoned, the Planning Department may 
dispose of and discard all documents, submissions and applications related to said 
application. The Town Building and Planning Administrator, or his or her 
designee, or the Chief Building Inspector shall provide writt en notice 30 days 
prior to expiration of the six -month period referenced above to the applicant 
informing said applicant of the Town Building and Planning Administrator's, or 
his or her designee's, or the Chief Building Inspector's  intent to deem the 
application abandoned. T h e  r e q u e s t  f o r  a n  e x t e n s i o n  o f  p r e l i m i n a r y

§ 301-255.1. Miscellaneous Provisions 
A. Signs erected by governmental authorities and/or related political subdivisions, excluding signs 
erected pursuant to and in discharge of any governmental function, law or regulation, shall 
comply with this chapter unless otherwise exempt under law or specifically waived by the 
Town Board, upon a recommendation from the Planning Department.

7.5.a
Packet Pg. 36
Attachment: Reso#194-Public Notice to Amend Chapter 301 Part 3 Article LI Wireless Communications Towers, Antennas, and Satellite Earth
 
 
§ 301-274. Permit required; applicability. 
A. No telecommunications tower or satellite earth station shall hereafter be used, erected, moved, 
reconstructed, changed, altered or modified to serve as a telecommunications tower or  
satellite earth station without the issuance of a special use permit(s) by the Town Board in 
conformity with the requirements of this article. 
B. Towers shall be permitted by special permit only in the following zoning use districts: APZ, 
PIP, PRP, RFC, DRC, SC, BC, CRC, Ind A CI, Ind C LI, RLC, and TRC, but shall not be 
permitted in whole or in part on any property used for residential purposes. 
C. Satellite earth stations shall by permitted by special permit only in the IND A CI, IND C LI, 
PIP and PD Zoning use districts, and shall not be permitted in whole or in part on any property 
used for residential purposes. 
D. New towers, antennas and satellite earth stations. All new towers, antennas and satellite earth 
stations in the Town shall be subject to these regulations, except as otherwise provided 
hereinbelow. 
E. Exceptions. The requirements set forth in this article shall not be applicable to: 
(1) Amateur radio operators' antennas and/or towers not exceeding 50 feet in height, which 
are owned and operated by a federally licensed amateur radio operator and which are 
located upon property that is the principal place of business or primary residence of the 
amateur radio operator. 
(2) Preexisting towers or antennas. 
(3) Residential satellite earth stations less than or equal to two meters in diameter. 
 
 
 
 
 
Underlines represent additions 
Strikethrough represents deletions

Instructions for Completing Part 1 
Part 1 is to be completed by the applicant or project sponsor.  Responses become part of the application for approval or funding, 
are subject to public review, and may be subject to further verification. 
Complete Part 1 based on information currently available.  If additional research or investigation would be needed to fully respond to 
any item, please answer as thoroughly as possible based on current information; indicate whether missing information does not exist, 
or is not reasonably available to the sponsor; and, when possible, generally describe work or studies which would be necessary to 
update or fully develop that information. 
Applicants/sponsors must complete all items in Sections A & B.  In Sections C, D & E, most items contain an initial question that 
must be answered either “Yes” or “No”. If the answer to the initial question is “Yes”, complete the sub-questions that follow.  If the 
answer to the initial question is “No”, proceed to the next question. Section F allows the project sponsor to identify and attach any 
additional information.  Section G requires the name and signature of the applicant or project sponsor to verify that the information 
contained in Part 1is accurate and complete.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
PUBLIC NOTICE 
 
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE, that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board 
of the Town of Riverhead, at 4 West Second Street , Riverhead, New York at its regular 
meeting held on March 4, 2025 at 2:00 p.m. to consider a Local Law to Amend Chapter 301 
Zoning and Land Development, Part 3 Supplementary Use Regulations , Article LII 
Commercial Solar Energy Production Systems , §301 -281 B. & C. Purposes; permitted 
districts; definitions. The intent of the proposed legislation is to implement recommendations 
of the 2024 Comprehensive Plan Update to remove Industrial A, Industrial B, and Industrial C 
and include Calverton Industrial and Light Industrial. 
 A copy of the entire text of the adopted local law and the provisions of the existing 
law to be amended may be reviewed at the Office of the Town Clerk, 4 W Second Street, 
Riverhead, New York 11901, between the hours of 8:30 a.m. and 4:30 p.m., Monday 
through Friday and can be accessed on the Town of Riverhead website at: 
www.townofriverheadny.gov under the Agenda and Minutes for the February 19, 2025  
Town Board Meeting.  
Dated:  Riverhead, New York 
   February 19, 2025  
 
 
BY ORDER OF THE TOWN BOARD 
OF THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
JAMES M. WOOTEN, TOWN CLERK 
 
7.6.a
Packet Pg. 51
Attachment: Reso#193-Public Notice to Amend Chapter 301 Part 3 Article LII Comercial Solar Energy Production Systems 301-281 Purpose
Downloaded from https://ecode360.com/RI0508 on 2025-01-13 
 
 
§ 301-281. Purpose; permitted districts; definitions.  
A. It is the intention of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead, as part of its goal to limit 
dependence on imported fossil energy and decrease greenhouse gas emissions, to permit 
commercial solar energy production systems in the industrial zoning use districts to minimize 
impacts to residents and scenic viewsheds important to the community. 
B. Commercial solar energy production systems shall be allowed with special permit approval 
by the Town Board in the Light Industrial (LI) Zoning Use District , Industrial A (Ind A) 
Zoning Use District, Industrial B District (General Industry) Calverton Industrial (CI) and the 
Planned Industrial Park (PIP) District. 
C. Commercial solar energy production systems shall be allowed with special permit approval 
by the Town Board in the Industrial C (Ind C) Light Industrial (LI) Zoning Use District that 
is located within the zip code boundary of Calverton. 
D. Definitions. As used in this section, the following terms shall have the meanings indicated: 
LOT COVERAGE — The lot coverage shall include the total square footage of the perimeter 
of all of the solar panels, inclusive of all interior spaces between the panels, in addition to 
driveways and service roads (paved or stone), and all accessory equipment, buildings and 
structures. 
 
 
 
 
 
Underlines represent additions 
Strikethrough represents deletions

Instructions for Completing Part 1 
Part 1 is to be completed by the applicant or project sponsor.  Responses become part of the application for approval or funding, 
are subject to public review, and may be subject to further verification. 
Complete Part 1 based on information currently available.  If additional research or investigation would be needed to fully respond to 
any item, please answer as thoroughly as possible based on current information; indicate whether missing information does not exist, 
or is not reasonably available to the sponsor; and, when possible, generally describe work or studies which would be necessary to 
update or fully develop that information. 
Applicants/sponsors must complete all items in Sections A & B.  In Sections C, D & E, most items contain an initial question that 
must be answered either “Yes” or “No”. If the answer to the initial question is “Yes”, complete the sub-questions that follow.  If the 
answer to the initial question is “No”, proceed to the next question. Section F allows the project sponsor to identify and attach any 
additional information.  Section G requires the name and signature of the applicant or project sponsor to verify that the information 
contained in Part 1is accurate and complete.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
PUBLIC NOTICE 
 
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE, that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board 
of the Town of Riverhead, at 4 West Second Street , Riverhead, New York at its regular 
meeting held on March 4, 2025 at 2:00 p.m. to consider a Local Law to Amend Chapter 301 
Zoning and Land Development, Part 3 Supplementary Use Regulations, Article LIID Battery 
Energy Storage Systems, §301-283.31 Requirements for Tier 2 battery energy storage 
systems. The intent of the proposed legislation is to implement recommendations of the 2024 
Comprehensive Plan Update to remove Industrial A and Industrial C and include Calverton 
Industrial and Light Industrial. 
 A copy of the entire text of the adopted local law and the provisions of the existing 
law to be amended may be reviewed at the Office of the Town Clerk, 4 W Second Street, 
Riverhead, New York 11901, between the hours of 8:30 a.m. and 4:30 p.m., Monday 
through Friday and can be accessed on the Town of Riverhead website at: 
www.townofriverheadny.gov under the Agenda and Minute s for the February 19, 2025  
Town Board Meeting.  
Dated:  Riverhead, New York 
   February 19, 2025  
 
 
BY ORDER OF THE TOWN BOARD 
OF THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
JAMES M. WOOTEN, TOWN CLERK

Part 1 - Project and Setting 
Instructions for Completing Part 1 
Part 1 is to be completed by the applicant or project sponsor.  Responses become part of the application for approval or funding, 
are subject to public review, and may be subject to further verification. 
Complete Part 1 based on information currently available.  If additional research or investigation would be needed to fully respond to 
any item, please answer as thoroughly as possible based on current information; indicate whether missing information does not exist, 
or is not reasonably available to the sponsor; and, when possible, generally describe work or studies which would be necessary to 
update or fully develop that information. 
Applicants/sponsors must complete all items in Sections A & B.  In Sections C, D & E, most items contain an initial question that 
must be answered either “Yes” or “No”. If the answer to the initial question is “Yes”, complete the sub-questions that follow.  If the 
answer to the initial question is “No”, proceed to the next question. Section F allows the project sponsor to identify and attach any 
additional information.  Section G requires the name and signature of the applicant or project sponsor to verify that the information 
contained in Part 1is accurate and complete.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD  
NOTICE OF PUBLIC HEARING  
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board of the 
Town of Riverhead at Riverhead Town Hall, 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York, on the 
4th day of March, 2025 at or about 2:10 p.m. to amend Chapter 229 of the Riverhead Town 
Code titled “Excavation and Grading”, Section 9 thereof, “Fees” The intent of the proposed 
amendment is to increase the excavation fees.  
 
 A copy of the entire text of the proposed local law and the provisions of the existing law to 
be amended may be reviewed at the Office of the Town Clerk, 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, 
New York 11901, between the hours of 8:30 a.m. and 4:30 p.m., Monday through Friday and can 
be accessed on the Town of Riverhead website at: www.townofriverheadny.gov under the Agenda 
and Minutes for the February 4, 2025 Town Board Meeting. 
Dated:  Riverhead, New York 
  February 4, 2025 
 
 
 BY THE ORDER OF THE TOWN BOARD 
 OF THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 JAMES M. WOOTEN, Town Clerk 
 
7.8.a
Packet Pg. 81
Attachment: Res. # 152 Notice of Public Hearing 229.9 Grading and Excavation Fees  (2025-15 : 2:10 PM Public Hearing Chapter 229-9
Chapter 229. Excavation and Grading 
Article I. Excavation 
§ 229-9 Fees. 
The Town Board or its designee shall charge and collect the following fees for excavation, exportation or 
importation pursuant to approved site plans, grading plans and realty subdivisions as required by 
Chapter 301, Zoning and Land Development. The officer designated by the Town Board to issue such 
permits shall charge and collect for each such permit a fee as follows. All fees are due and owing and 
shall be paid at the time of issuance of the permit. Premises that qualify for one or more of the 
delineated exemptions in § 229-4 shall not be assessed any fees pursuant to this section. 
A.  For residential, commercial and industrial subdivision, site plans or grading plans, a fee shall be 
imposed in the amount of $2 3.00 per cubic yard for all material removed from or returned to 
the site in accordance with Town requirements for drainage, parking and other Town-required 
improvements and also for any and all purposes and improvements other than those required 
for compliance with Town requirements. The determination of the fee to be paid shall be made 
by the Town Board or the Planning Board or their designee subsequent to a review of the 
estimate submitted.

 WHEREAS, pursuant to Town Law, § 64(8), the Town Board is expressly 
authorized to accept a gift “. . . for any public use, upon such terms or conditions as may 
be prescribed by the grantor or donor and accepted by said town, and provide for the 
proper administration of the same”; and 
 
 WHEREAS, the Town Board finds that acceptance of the roses with an 
approximate value of $625.00 to the Town for the Riverhead Senior Center is in the best 
interest of the residents of the Town of Riverhead. 
 
 NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED , that the Town of Riverhead hereby 
accepts the generous donation of the roses with an approximate value of $625.00 (Six 
Hundred Twenty -Five Do llars and 00/100) from Gabrielsen Farms to the Town of 
Riverhead for the Riverhead Senior Center; and be it further, 
 
 RESOLVED that a copy of this resolution shall be forwarded to the Office of the 
Town Attorney, the Accounting Department and the Riverhea d Senior Center; and be it 
further, 
 
 RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE

TB Resolution 2025-215 
 
AUTHORIZES SEWER DISTRICT EMPLOYEE TO ATTEND SEMINAR 
 
Councilman Kern offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Merrifield 
 
WHEREAS, SUNY Morrisville is sponsoring Wastewater Treatment Operators 
Certification Courses having a specific course entitled, “Basic Laboratory Procedures” to 
be held on May 5, 2025 through May 9, 2025; and 
WHEREAS, it is the desire of Michael Reichel, Sewer District Superintendent, 
that Sewer District employee # GFZ001293 attend such course and that such course is 
not for promotional or change of position purposes but instead is for and in furtherance 
of said employee’s current position; and 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board of the Town of 
Riverhead hereby authorizes Sewer District employee # GFZ001293 to attend the 
aforementioned course to be held at SUNY Morrisville on May 5, 2025 through May 9, 
2025 for and in furtherance of employee’s current position; and be it further subject to 
the condition that in the event the employee leaves Town service within two years of 
their hire date or an employee with more than two years of service leaves Town service 
within one year from the date of the training described above, the employee shall be 
required to reimburse the District for the cost and expense of the training program or at 
the District’s option the training cost and expense may be deducted from their earnings, 
via regular pay or SCAT (vacation, sick, etc.); and be it further 
RESOLVED, that all related, receipted, expenses incurred by the Sewer District 
employee, not to exceed a total cost of $2,552.00, and the employee shall complete the 
Training Reimbursement Agreement prior to attendance of conference/travel, and 
subject to completion of the Training Reimbursement Agreement the employee shall be 
reimbursed upon their return in accordance with the Town of Riverhead Policy; and be it 
further resolved 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE

and 
 
 WHEREAS, since 2005 and for several years, the Small Business Advisory 
Committee did meet and advise the Town Board on various matters related to business 
and members participate in meetings and roundtable discussions highlighting a variety 
of business issues unique to East End of Long Island; and 
 
 WHEREAS, the By-Laws of the Town of Riverhead Small Business Advisory 
Committee adopted on August 16 state there shall be not less than nine nor more than 
thirteen members appointed by the Town Board and all members shall have voting rights and 
the members appointed are to serve staggered terms of one year and two years; and 
 
 WHEREAS, Connie Lassandro, Lee Mendelsen, Monique Parsons, Steve 
Shauger and Tracy Stark-James, were reappointed by Resolution #2024-616 on July2, 
2024, to fulfill a holdover term which expired on December 31st, 2024; and 
 
 WHEREAS, Monique Parsons will be the committee chair; and 
 
 WHEREAS, Dean Del Prete has expressed interest to fill a vacancy; and 
 
 WHEREAS, the Town Board wishes to appoint Dean Del Prete, and reappoint 
Diane Burke, Connie Lassandro, Lee Mendelsen, Monique Parsons as chairperson, 
Steve Shauger and Tracy Stark-James to the Town of Riverhead Small Business 
Advisory Committee for the remainder of a one (1) year term which will expire 
December 31, 2025. 
 
 NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED that the Town Board appoints Dean Del 
Prete, and reappoints Diane Burke, Connie Lassandro, Lee Mendelsen, Monique 
Parsons as chairperson, Steve Shauger and Tracy Stark-James to the Town of 
Riverhead Small Business Advisory Committee for the remainder of a one (1) year term 
which will expire December 31, 2025; and be it further

resolution to the Town Board Coordinator, who shall distribute to the aforementioned 
committee member; and be it further

Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, on October 14, 1997, the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead  
adopted Local Law No. 14-1997, known and cited as the “Agricultural Lands 
Preservation Law of the Town of Riverhead“ for the purpose of preserving prime 
agricultural land and maintenance of a viable agricultural industry in the Town of 
Riverhead; and    
 
WHEREAS, such local law provided for the creation of a Farmland Preservation 
Committee, its composition and its authority; and 
 
WHEREAS, such local law empowers the Town Board to appoint members to 
the Farmland Preservation Committee; and   
 
WHEREAS, a vacancy does exist on the Farmland Preservation Committee; and  
 
WHEREAS, the Town Board wishes to appoint Ken Zilnicki to the Farmland 
Preservation Committee for a two-year term that will expire December 31, 2026. 
   
NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board hereby appoints 
Ken Zilnicki to the Farmland Preservation Committee for a two-year term that will expire 
January 15, 2026; and be it further

resolution to the Office of the Town Attorney; and be it further  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.

TB Resolution 2025-221 
 
RATIFIES THE APPOINTMENT OF WASTEWATER TREATMENT PLANT 
OPERATOR TRAINEES 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, Joseph Hartmann has been serving as a provisional appointment in 
the position of Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator Trainee since January 16, 2024; 
and 
WHEREAS, Caeser Quesada has been serving as a provisional appointment in 
the position of Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator Trainee since June 2, 2024; and 
 
WHEREAS, on December 27, 2024 the Suffolk County Department of Civil 
Service established a certified List of Eligibles, list 24AF810, for the three (3) vacancies 
in the position of Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator Trainee; and  
 
WHEREAS, Civil Service regulations require that a permanent appointment of a 
provisional employee be made within sixty days of the date a Certified List of Eligibles is 
first established.   
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that pursuant to Civil Service 
regulations, this Town Board hereby removes the provisional status of Joseph 
Hartmann and Caeser Quesada and appoints each to the title of Wastewater Treatment 
Plant Operator Trainee effective February 25, 2025 at no change to their current

03.04.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-222 
 
RATIFIES THE APPOINTMENT OF AN AUTOMOTIVE EQUIPMENT OPERATOR 
 
Councilman Rothwell offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Kern 
 
WHEREAS, pursuant to Town Law § 64(1), the Town Board has general 
management and control of the finances of the Town; and 
 WHEREAS, pursuant to Town Law § 64(3), the Town Board has general 
management and control of Town property; and  
WHEREAS, pursuant to Town Law § 20 and except as otherwise provided by 
law, the Town Board has the responsibility to employ such persons as the Town Board 
deems necessary for the proper conduct of the affairs of the Town; and 
WHEREAS, pursuant to Town Law § 27, the Town Board shall fix, from time to 
time, the salaries of all officers, officials and employees of said town, whether elected or 
appointed, and determine when the same shall be payable; and   
WHEREAS, pursuant to Highway Law § 140(4), the Highway Superintendent 
shall employ such persons as may be necessary for the maintenance and repair of 
Town highways and removal of obstructions caused by snow and provide for the 
supervision over such employees, subject to the provisions of law recited above and, 
including but not limited to, available appropriations for such purpose, any applicable 
civil service requirements; and  
WHEREAS, the Highway Superintendent filed a Personnel Report and Request 
for Town Board Resolution to Effectuate Personnel Request, to wit appointment of 
Steven Sostre to the position of Automotive Equipment Operator effective March 3, 
2025; and 
WHEREAS, the Highway Superintendent’s report stated that said appointment is 
necessary for the repair and maintenance of Town highways; and 
WHEREAS, this position was duly posted in accordance with the terms of the 
CSEA contract, Job Posting #1 of 2025.  
NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board accepts the 
Highway Superintendent’s Personnel Report and Request Town Board Resolution to 
Effectuate Personnel Request, to wit:  the appointment of Steven Sostre effective March 
3, 2025 to the position of Automotive Equipment Operator and sets his salary at Group 
6, Step 4A of the CSEA Operational and Technical Salary Schedule which is 
$55,306.57 per annum; and be it further

Superintendent; and be it further      
 RESOLVED that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
resolution to the Town Highway Superintendent, Personnel Officer, Financial 
Administrator, Payroll and Town Attorney’s Office; and be it further   
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.

TB Resolution 2025-225 
 
APPROVES SALARY ADJUSTMENTS FOR MUNICIPAL GARAGE MECHANICS 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, the 2025 budget for the municipal garage was based on the 2024 
employees and their expected salaries and after such was adopted, an employee gave 
their notice to retire, leaving additional funds in the personnel budget line for municipal 
garage; and 
 
WHEREAS, in an attempt to attract and retain diesel mechanics, it is in the best 
interest of the Town to use those already budgeted funds to adjust the salaries of the 
existing mechanics as well as the one vacancy to try and better reach market value; and  
 
WHEREAS, the Town Supervisor did meet with the Department Head, Ken 
Testa, to review and discuss the request for the salary increase; and 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, the Town Board hereby approves an 
increase in annual salary effective March 9, 2025 with no other change to the terms or 
conditions of employment. The current and new salaries are found on the Operational & 
Technical salary schedule and are outlined below.  
 
 
  
 
  
  
  
BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, a copy of this be forwarded to payroll and all 
Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this resolution from the 
electronic storage device and if needed, a certified copy of same from the Office of the 
Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-227 
 
AUTHORIZES THE SUPERVISOR TO EXECUTE A LICENSE AGREEMENT WITH 
BROADCAST MUSIC, INC. (BMI) 
 
Councilman Kern offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Merrifield 
 
WHEREAS, the Town of Riverhead plays pre-recorded music in the form of 
compact discs, digital video discs, cassettes, and other media in Town facilities and at 
Town events (e.g. the senior center, teen activities); and  
 
WHEREAS, many of these works are protected by U.S. Copyright Law; and  
 
WHEREAS, a municipality requires permission from the holders of such 
copyrights to use the works in a public forum; and  
 
WHEREAS, Broadcast Music, Inc. (BMI) represents the holders of copyrights for 
over 8 million such works; and  
 
WHEREAS, BMI offers a license granting permission to municipalities to play all 
of the works of copyright holders BMI represents; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Town of Riverhead wishes to execute a license agreement with 
BMI for the right to play pre-recorded music represented by BMI for the period January 
1, 2025 to December 31, 2025 in the amount of $446.00. 
 
NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Supervisor is hereby 
authorized to execute a license agreement with BMI for the right to play pre-recorded 
music represented by BMI in substantially the form annexed hereto; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
resolution to the office of the Town Attorney; and be it further  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.  
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
SECONDER: Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
AYES: Kenneth Rothwell, Robert Kern, Denise Merrifield, Joann Waski 
ABSENT: Tim Hubbard

AUTHORIZES THE SUPERVISOR TO EXECUTE LEASE RENEWAL AGREEMENT 
AUTHORIZING THE TOWN TO LEASE A VEHICLE FROM SUFFOLK COUNTY 
OFFICE FOR THE AGING FOR TRANSPORTATION SERVICES FOR ELDERLY 
RESIDENTS, NUNC PRO TUNC 
 
Councilwoman Merrifield offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Waski 
 
WHEREAS, the Senior Citizen Department offers a wide variety of programs, 
activities and support services including transportation services  to the elderly residents 
of the Riverhead community; and   
 
WHEREAS, Resolution #750 adopted on September 21, 2010 authorized a 
Lease Agreement between the Town of Riverhead and Suffolk County Office for the 
Aging regarding lease of vehicle for use by the  Town of Riverhead for transportation 
services to the elderly residents of the Town; and  
 
WHEREAS, Resolution #708 adopted on October 6, 2015 authorized extension 
of the Lease Agreement regarding lease of vehicle for transportation services to the 
elderly residents of the Town through December 31, 2019; and  
 
WHEREAS, Resolution #2020 -223 adopted on May 5, 2020 authorized 
extension of the Lease Agreement regarding lease of vehicle for transportation services 
to the elderly residents of the Town through December 31, 2024; and  
 
WHEREAS, both parties are interested in renewing the Lease Agreement for 
vehicle to be used by the Senior Citizen Department to transport elderly residents of the 
Riverhead community. 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that the Supervisor is hereby authorized 
to execute the attached Lease Renewal Agreement with Suffolk County Office for the 
Aging, nunc pro tunc, authorizing the Town of Riverhead to accept a vehicle to transport 
elderly residents of the Town of Riverhead for One Dollar ($1. 00) per year from January 
1, 2025 to December 31, 2029, payment waived; and be it further   
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
resolution to the Office of the Town Attorney; and be it further 
  
RESOLVED, that all To wn Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.

03.04.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-229 
 
RATIFIES AUTHORIZATION TO PURCHASE CALRES 2109 FOR THE WATER 
DISTRICT 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, the Riverhead Water District has a Calgon water treatment system 
at Plant 16 designed to operate with CalRes 2109 resin as a filtering media, with 
internal screens designed to contain the grain size of CalRes 2109, with said system 
and its design and filtering media approved by New York State Department of Health; 
and  
 
WHEREAS, CalRes 2109 is solely available for purchase from Calgon Carbon 
Corporation, and the Town Purchasing Agent has investigated and confirmed the 
designation of Calgon Carbon Corporation as a sole source for CalRes 2109 and that 
such purchase complies with GML §103; and 
 
WHEREAS, the total cost of a complete exchange of CalRes2109 including 
delivery and loading of the new media, and removal and disposal of the old media is 
$186,000.00; and 
 
WHEREAS, due to the large dollar value of this sole source purchase, the Town 
Purchasing Agent is bringing this information to the Town Board and seeking Town 
Board authorization to execute the purchase order; and 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that the Purchasing Agent is authorized 
to purchase CalRes 2109 from Calgon Carbon Corporation for use in the Calgon water 
treatment system at Plant 16 at a total cost of $186,000.00 and to execute a Purchase 
Order for same; and 
 
BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk be and is hereby authorized 
to forward a copy of this resolution to the Purchasing Department and the Water District; 
and 
 
BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED that all Town Hall Departments may review and 
obtain a copy of this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a 
certified copy of same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE

adopt rules of procedure for conducting Town Board meetings; and 
 
 WHEREAS, by Resolution # 186, adopted on March 5, 2013, The Town Board of 
the Town of Riverhead adopted rules and procedures for Riverhead Town Board 
meetings; and

of the Town of Riverhead adopted rules and procedures for Riverhead Town Board 
meetings; and

Board meetings; and

the adopted rules and procedures for Riverhead Town Board meetings.

-1- 
RULES OF THE TOWN BOARD OF THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
DEFINITIONS 
 
“Regular Meeting” or “Special Meeting” shall mean a gathering of a quorum of the 
Riverhead Town Board at which time motions, proposals, resolutions and any other matter 
may be formally discussed and debated and/or a vote taken thereon. 
 
“Work Session” shall mean a gathering of a quorum of the Riverhead Town Board at which 
time, matters and resolutions will be informally discussed and no vote shall be taken on 
such matters. 
 
RULE I.  REGULAR MEETINGS 
 
The Town Board shall meet as established by resolution by  the Town Board.  Except as 
otherwise set forth in said resolution of the Town Board, the Town Board shall meet on the 
first and third Tuesdays of each month alternating between a start time of 2:00 PM and 
6:00 PM; except that in January, when the first To wn Board meeting will be either on the 
first Wednesday or Thursday at 2:00 PM immediately following the January 1 st holiday 
and any regular meeting which would fall on a Tuesday following an observed holiday for 
which Town Hall was closed shall be instead held on the Wednesday following such 
holiday.   
 
RULE II. WORK SESSIONS 
 
Work Session meetings will be held, weekly, on Thursdays commencing at 10:00 AM and 
shall be informal. In no event, except exigent and/or emergency circumstances shall Work 
Session be held less than twice each month.    
 
Work Session Agenda : A proposed written agenda shall be prepared for each Work 
Session Meeting and shall be distributed, together with any items to be considered at the 
meeting to the members of the Town Board , the Town Attorney, the Town Board 
Coordinator, the Town Clerk and any other department head with an item on the agenda 
no later than 4:30 p.m. on the Tuesday preceding the scheduled meeting  and in the event 
amendments are made to the Agenda, the Amended Agenda shall be recirculated as soon 
as practicable upon amendment. 
 
Town Board m embers, the Town Attorney ’s Office, the Plannin g Administrator, Town 
Clerk, Chief of Police, Town Engineer, Highway Superintendent and Town Financial 
Administrator and any other Town Department Head may make requests to add discussion 
items to the Work Session Agenda which shall be submitted no later than 2:30 p.m. on the 
day preceding the scheduled meeting.  The Supervisor’s Office shall send, either in writing 
or by electronic transmission a copy of the revised and final Work Session Agenda to the 
Town Board Members, the Town Board Coordinator, the Town Attorney, the Town Clerk 
and any other department head with a discussion item on the Agenda and cause same to be 
posted upon the Town’s website.  
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 150
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-2- 
 
During a Work Session Meeting or Regular Town Board Meeting , the Town Board may 
elect to move into an Executive Session as provided under Public Officers Law section 
105.  Subject matters that shall be considered confidential or privileged when discussed in 
an Executive Session are as follows:  
 
i. Matters which would imperil public safety if disclosed. 
ii. Any matter which may disclose the identity of a law enforcement agent or 
informer. 
iii. Information relating to current or future investigation or prosecution of a 
criminal offense which would imperil effective law enforcement if 
disclosed. 
iv. Proposed, pending or current litigation. 
v. The medical, financial, credit or employment history of any person or 
corporation, or matters leading to the appointment, employment, 
promotion, demotion, discipline, suspension, dismissal or removal of any 
person. 
vi. Collective Bargaining Negotiations. 
vii. The proposed acquisition, sale or lease of real property or the proposed 
acquisition of securities, or sale or exchange of securities held by such 
public body, but only when publicity would substantially affect the value 
thereof.  
 
The Town Supervisor shall assign the various Town Board Members as liaisons to Departments 
of the Town Government and Town Hall Advisory Committees. At least monthly, Heads of 
Departments shall be scheduled to appear and report o n and/or discuss matters of significance to 
and within the Department under their charge.  The Town Attorney shall be present to advise on 
any matters and/or discussions that should, due to subject matter thereof, more properly be referred 
to an Executive Session discussion.  Additionally, Town Hall Advisory Committees shall be 
scheduled to appear and report on and/or discuss matters of significance to such committees at 
least once every three (3) months/quarter.  In the event a matter has been referred to an Advisory 
Committee by the Town Board, said Committee, or a representative thereof, together with the 
assigned Town Board liaison should be scheduled to appear at a Work Session for discussion 
promptly following the Advisory Committee’s first meeting following referral of a matter.  
 
 
RULE III. SPECIAL MEETINGS 
 
Special meetings shall meet at the call of the  Town Clerk upon direction of the Town  
Supervisor or upon the filing with the Town Clerk a written request by any two members 
of the Town Board.  At such special meeting, no business other than that named in the  
public notice of the meeting shall be transacted.    Written Notice of the Special Meeting 
shall be given as soon as practicable after such meeting is duly scheduled in accordance 
herewith but in no event less than twenty -four (24) hours prior to the commencement of 
such meeting.   
 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 151
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-3- 
A Special Meeting cannot be held until each Town Board Member has bee n duly served 
with a notice of such Special Meeting  in writing (in -hand, personal delivery, email or 
facsimile), including notice of the date, time and place for the Special Meeting as well as 
a list of the items to be discussed at such Special Meeting, no  later than twenty-four (24) 
hours prior to such meeting.   Town Board members may waive notice of the meeting in 
writing. 
 
This Rule III may only be suspended by affirmative, unanimous vote of all Members of the Town 
Board and to the extent permitted by law. 
  
RULE IV. CONDUCT OF MEETINGS & QUORUM AT REGULAR MEETINGS 
 
All Regular and Special Meetings and all Work Sessions of the Town Board shall be held 
in the Town Hall Meeting Room located at 4 West Second Street , Riverhead, New York 
11901 or any such physical location to which the Riverhead Town Hall is relocated 
subsequent to the adoption of these rules.  All meetings shall be conducted in accordance 
with the New York State Open Meetings Law.  The Town Clerk shall keep formal minutes 
for all Regular and Special Meetings.   
 
The attendance of a majority of the Town Board shall constitute a quorum, subject to any 
requirements of virtual attendance and participation authorized by the Riverhead Town 
Code. 
 
The Town Attorney shall act as Parliamentarian at Regular and Special Meetings of the 
Town Board and shall assist and advise on all questions of procedure upon request of any 
member of the Town Board. 
 
This Rule IV may only be suspended by affirmative, unanimous vote of all Members of the Town 
Board and only to the extent allowed by State or County Law. 
 
RULE V. PRESIDING OFFICER 
 
The Supervisor shall preside as the Chair at all meetings of the Town Board, but in his/her 
absence or inability to serve, the Deputy Supervisor shall act as presiding officer, and shall 
so serve until the return of the Supervisor.  In the event that neither the Supervisor, nor the 
Deputy Supervi sor shall be present to preside at a meeting, the Town Board members 
present shall nominate and elect a temporary chair.   
 
The presiding officer shall possess the following power and perform the following duties: 
 
1. He/she shall preserve order and decorum during the meeting as further 
discussed in Rule VI.  
2. He/she shall set the agenda which may include the order in which duly 
submitted resolutions are called upon for action.  
 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 152
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-4- 
This Rule V may only be suspended by affirmative, unanimous vote of all Memb ers of the Town 
Board to the extent permitted by law. 
 
 
RULE VI.  DECORUM AT REGULAR MEETINGS 
 
A. The Supervisor or other presiding officer shall convene the Town Board promptly at the 
appointed hour.  The Supervisor shall recognize any Town Board member for the purpose 
of debate or comment on any matter under consideration, in the order in which recognition 
has been requested .  The Supervisor shall decide all questions of order, which decision 
shall be final unless appealed to the Members of Town B oard and thereafter overruled by 
majority vote. 
 
B. Signs, signboards, posters, banners , flyers and the like shall not be permitted at 
meetings of the Town Board. Distribution of flyers in the meeting room is also not 
permitted.  Such instruments serve to distract, disrupt and/or obstruct viewing of 
the meeting and given the opportunities to speak before the Town Board on a 
variety of matters do not substantively c ontribute to the business of the Town 
Board. 
 
C. Speakers from the audience, at appropriate times hereafter defined, shall address 
the Town Board as a whole, in an orderly manner.  All Speakers, including the 
Supervisor and members of the Town Board shall refrain from  personal, 
impertinent, slanderous, vulgar, inflammatory, threatening, and/or profane remarks 
directed at any member of the Board, town staff, general public, applicants before 
the Board , other attendees and/or invited guests.  Further, racial, ethnic and/or 
sexual slurs, at any time, directed to any person are prohibited.   Any person , 
including recognized speakers, who makes such remarks or otherwise disrupts the 
meeting with loud outbursts, shouting, threats or other disruptive conduct or 
behavior shall, at the direction of the Supervisor or after a motion and majority 
consensus of the Town Board, be ruled out of order and receive a warning.  If, after 
receiving a warning, any person persists in disrupting the meeting  and failing to 
maintain decorum, the Supervisor or Town Board majority shall order that person 
to leave the meeting.  In the event that an individual ordered to remove themselves 
from the meeting fails to comply with the Chair’s directive, law enforcement 
personnel may be utilized to enforce such order of removal.  Criticism of Town 
policies, procedures, programs, or services or acts or omissions of the Town Board 
shall not be considered improper unless the speaker fails to maintain decorum and 
courtesy, including refraining from personal, impertinent, slanderous , vulgar, 
inflammatory, threatening, racial, e thnic and/or sexual slurs and/o r profane 
remarks, whereupon the Chair of the meeting may call such speaker to order as set 
forth hereinabove. 
 
This Rule VI may only be suspended by affirmative, unanimous vote of all Members of the Town 
Board. 
 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 153
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-5- 
 
 
RULE VII. ORDER OF BUSINESS 
 
1. Roll Call, which may be dispensed with if there is no question as to whether a 
quorum is present for the conduct of official business 
2. Pledge of Allegiance to the Flag of the United States of America which shall not be 
dispensed with at any meeting. 
3. Invocation by member of the faith community, or if none present, by any attendee at 
the invitation of the Chair of the meeting. 
4. Public Presentation/Agenda Items 
5. Approval of the Minutes of the preceding meeting(s) 
6. Miscellaneous Communications 
7. Committee Reports 
8. Public Hearings 
9. Discussion Items, if any 
10. Public comment on Resolutions 
11. Call of & Action Upon Resolutions  
12. Public Comment on any matters of concern to the Town 
13. Adjournment 
 
 
RULE VIII. PUBLIC HEARINGS 
 
Public Hearings shall be scheduled on the Agenda and noticed at staggered intervals in the order 
set by the Town Board at a preceding Regular Meeting or Special Meeting called for the purpose 
of setting such public hearing.  To the extent feasible, the Town Board shall endeavor to schedule 
public hearings on proposed Local Laws, amendments to Local Laws and land use applications at 
Meetings scheduled to begin at 6:00 post -meridian.  The Town Board shall endeavor to limit the 
scheduling of public hearings to three (3) such hearin gs per Regular Meeting.  Comment and 
Decorum at and during Public Hearings are addressed elsewhere herein. 
 
The Town Board may vote on any public hearing matter for which all speakers have been 
accommodated, providing that no person affirmatively opposes  subject matter of the Public 
Hearing and sets forth substantive reasons therefor and the hearing is then closed by the Supervisor.  
If someone does so speak against the subject matter of the hearing, all hearing decisions shall be 
reserved until at least the next Regular Meeting or Special Meeting of the Board to permit sufficient 
time to allow comment to be evaluated. 
 
The Town Supervisor or, in the alternative, a majority of the Town Board, may elect to leave the 
hearing open for the submission of written comment to a date certain but no more than ten (10) 
days.  In such case, the Board may not vote on the subject matter until the Regular Meeting or any 
duly called Special Town Board Meeting following the end of the period for submission of written 
comment. 
 
 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 154
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-6- 
 
 
RULE IX. PERMISSION FOR PUBLIC TO SPEAK BEFORE THE TOWN BOARD 
 
A.  COMMENTS ON RESOLUTIONS 
 
Prior to the introduction Resolutions, the Supervisor may allow any member of the 
audience to speak once for not more than 3 minutes in relation to all Resolutions which are 
on the agenda, but not scheduled for Public Hearings.  Speakers shall state their name, 
hamlet within the Town in which they reside or, if not a Town resident, sufficiently identify 
the area or Town from which they hail or the group o r person on behalf of whom they 
intend to speak.  Speakers shall not be permitted to “yield” their time to other speakers.  
Speakers shall offer comment specific to a resolution/s appearing on the Agenda and shall 
so identify such resolution/s at the beginning of their comment.  Speakers shall refrain from 
reading written comments submitted by others and such written comments shall be instead 
submitted to the Town Clerk to be incorporated into the minutes and distributed t o the 
members of the Town Board. Speakers are encouraged to concisely address the issue on 
which they are to be heard and refrain from repeating themselves. Speakers may appear via 
ZOOM or other videoconferencing application. Decorum shall be maintained as set forth 
in Rule VI hereinabove.  
 
B.  COMMENTS DURING PUBLIC HEARINGS 
 
Any person attending the meeting may speak at Public Hearings once per public hearing. 
There shall be no  set time limit for “publi c comment” at Public Hearings  and instead the 
Chair shall exercise discre tion to uniformly limit the duration of comments , and such 
discretion should typically be reserved for heavily attended hearings where time limitations 
serve to conduct the hearing in a timely and efficient manner. The Chair shall further have 
discretion to limit the number of opportunities to speak during public hearings, but such 
discretion shall be exercised uniformly during a particular public hearing.  Speakers shall 
state their name, hamlet within the Town in w hich they reside or, if not a Town resident, 
sufficiently identify the area or Town from which they hail and/or the group or person on 
behalf of whom they intend to speak. Speakers shall refrain from reading written comments 
submitted by others which written comments shall be instead submitted to the Town Clerk 
to be incorporated into the minutes and distributed to the members of the Town Board.  
Decorum shall be maintained as set forth in Rule V hereinabove. Speakers may appear via 
ZOOM or other videoconfe rencing application as made available by the Department of 
Information and Technology and speakers appearing via videoconference shall be subject 
to the Rules of Decorum as set forth herein at Rule VI above. 
 
 
Public Hearings relate to specific subject matter before the Town Board for consideration 
and accordingly, all comments offered during public hearings shall be pertinent to such 
subject matter.  If, at any time, a speaker’s comments are deemed to be impertinent to the 
subject of the hearing and/or unn ecessarily repetitive of the speaker’s own prior remarks 
or comments the Chair may rule and direct the speaker to yield the floor to the next speaker, 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 155
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-7- 
or if there being no further speaker/s, close the hearing.  The ruling of the Chair may be 
appealed to the Town Board which appeal shall require a majority of the Town Board to 
overrule.   
 
Questions of relevance shall be referred to and determined by the Parliamentarian. 
Decorum shall be maintained as set forth in Rule VI herein above. 
 
C.  PUBLIC COMMENTS ON ANY MATTERS RELEVANT TO THE TOWN 
OF RIVERHEAD 
 
Members of the audience may also address the Town Board on any subject once during the 
“public comment” period and such comments shall be limited to not more than 3 minutes 
and shall be substantively relevant to issues concerning the Town of Riverhead.   Speakers 
shall state their name, hamlet within the Town in which they reside or, if not a Town 
resident, sufficiently identify the area or Town from which they hail or the group or person 
on behalf of whom they intend to speak. Speakers shall not be permitted to “yield ” their 
time to other speakers. Speakers shall refrain from reading written comments submitted by 
others and such written comments shall be instead submitted to  the Town Clerk to be 
incorporated into the minutes and distributed to the members of the Town Board.  No 
member of the public shall engage in any disruptive demonstration or otherwise disrupt the 
formality of a Town Board meeting.  Speakers will be requir ed to address their remarks 
exclusively to the Town Board without engaging the general public in debate. Speakers are 
encouraged to concisely address the issue on which they are to be heard and refrain from 
repeating themselves. Speakers may appear via ZOO M or other videoconferencing 
application. Decorum shall be maintained as set forth in Rule VI hereinabove.   
 
This Rule IX may only be suspended by affirmative, unanimous vote of all Members of the Town 
Board. 
 
 
RULE X. DEBATE 
 
 The rules governing debate shall be as follows: 
 
A. Debate shall not begin on a Local Law, Resolution or otherwise debatable 
motion until it has been moved by a Town Board member and seconded by 
another Town Board member. 
 
B. The Supervisor may offer or second a resolution or a motion and need not 
relinquish the chair for such purpose. 
 
C. Members of the Town Board wishing to speak shall first address th e Chair of 
the Meeting and gain recognition whereupon they shall have the floor and 
Board Members so speaking shall confine comments to the question, resolution 
or action under debate.   
 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 156
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-8- 
D. No Board member shall speak more than once on any questions until ev ery 
member choosing to speak shall have spoken, nor more than twice in any case 
without leave of the Board. 
 
E. During Debate and/or consideration of a question, resolution or action, any 
Member of the Board  after receiving recognition by the Chair, call upon  and 
address questions to Town Staff and Officials relative to the question, resolution 
or action under debate.   
 
F. Once recognized by the Chair of the Meeting, a Town Member to whom the 
floor has been given shall not suffer interruption except upon being c alled to 
Order by the Chair, a point of order or point of personal privilege is raised by 
another Member of the Board, or the speaker yields to a question by another 
Board Member. 
 
G. Once recognized, the Member of the Board speaking shall hold the floor until 
the conclusion of that member’s remarks and this shall include any Town Staff 
or Official called upon by said Member. 
 
H. All Points of Order shall be determined by the Chair of the Meeting whose 
decision shall be final unless appeal be made to and overruled by a majority of 
the Town Board present.  The Parliamentarian may be called upon to assist in 
the determination of a Point of Order. 
 
I. Points of Personal Privilege shall be the right of a Member of the Town Board 
to address the Board on matters which directly relate to matters or questions of 
that Member’s integrity, character and/or motives.  Members of the Board 
raising a Point of Personal Privilege shall be permitted to interrupt a speaker to 
whom the floor has been given whereupon debate shall be suspended until such 
time as the Point of Personal Privilege has been determined by the 
Parliamentarian.   
 
J. Members of the Public or audience present at the Meeting shall have no right 
to raise Points of Order or of Personal Privilege, except as set forth in Rule IX, 
subparagraphs “A” and “C” above.  
 
RULE XI. DEBATABLE MOTIONS 
 
 Debatable motions shall be as follows: 
 
A. The Main Motion .  The main motion is a motion by itself or one to adopt a 
Local Law or Resolution before the Town Board.  It may be amended and 
requires a majority vote except where otherwise required by law or these rules.  
A motion may be withdrawn by its proposer at any time before a vote is taken. 
 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 157
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-9- 
B. An Amendment to the Main Motion or an Amendment of Such 
Amendment.  An amendment is a motion to change or modify the main motion 
or an amendment of it.  An amendment shall not be amended more than once.  
Amendments shall be disposed of in inverse order before voting on the main 
motion and requires a majority vote. 
 
C. To Commit.  This motion is used to refer a matter to committee or Town Staff 
or back to committee or Town Staff.  The motion may be amended and requires 
a majority vote. 
 
RULE XII. MOTIONS WITHOUT DEBATE 
 
 The following motions are not debatable: 
 
A. To Table  or Un -Table.  This motion is used to postpone a subject under 
discussion to a time in the near future.  This motion is not amendable and must 
carry by a  majority vote.  When a subject  previously tabled  is to be 
reconsidered, a motion is offered to remove the matter from the table and such 
motion is similarly not amendable, nor debatable .  Once removed from the 
“Table”, the subject is treated as a “Main Motion”. 
 
B. To Adjourn.  The Chair may adjourn the meeting when all agenda items are 
completed.  A Board member may also move to adjourn.  This motion is always 
in order except when a speaker has the floor, during roll call or immediately 
after it has been voted down.  It requires a majority vote. 
 
C. The Previous Question.  This motion is used to close debate and may be made 
by any Town Board member when debate has become long and drawn out.  It 
is made in the following manner: “Mr. Supervisor, I move the previous 
question.” Without a second, the presiding officer then asks the Town Board 
members, “Shall debate be  closed and the question now be put?”  The Clerk 
then calls the full roll, and if the majority of those present vote in the 
affirmative, the question under debate and then before the Town Board 
members is immediately voted upon in the usual manner without further debate. 
If the majority of those present decline the motion, debate resumes in the normal 
course.  Each Town Board Member may make this motion only once with 
respect to debate over a matter and such a motion may only be offered when a 
speaker’s remarks have concluded. 
 
 
RULE XIII. PROCEDURE ON LOCAL LAWS 
 
The adoption of a LOCAL LAW or an amendment thereto requires the affirmative vote of 
at least a majority of all the members of the Town Board. No LOCAL LAW shall be 
adopted e xcept at a duly noticed Regular or Spec ial Meeting of the Town Board and 
LOCAL LAWS shall not be adopted by ratification. A LOCAL LAW amended after 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 158
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-10- 
introduction does no t become a new LOCAL LAW requiring another Public Hearing 
unless the amendment constitutes and is ruled a substantial change by the Chairman.   
“Substantial” shall, at minimum, mean a textual change that materially alters the intent or 
foreseeable practical effect of the LOCAL LAW.  “Substantial” shall not include spelling, 
grammar, or other typographical errors.  This Rule XIII shall not be suspended by the Town 
Board. 
 
 
RULE XIV. PROCEDURE ON RESOLUTIONS 
 
Except as otherwise provided by law, the passage of a Resolution requires the affirmative 
vote of a majority of the members present at the meeting which action is taken. 
 
Any resolution to be introduced by any Town Board member at a scheduled meeting of the 
Town Board shall be filed in the office of the Town Clerk by 4:00 PM on the business day 
prior to said Town Board meeting.  Any resolutions legally submitted to the Town Clerk 
that were not presented at work -session and that will be presented at the Town Board 
meeting shall be delivered to each Board Member as soon as possible after being submitted 
to the Town Clerk. 
 
Further, where said Town Board meeting is to commence at a time other than 2:00 PM or  
6:00 PM (alternating), any Resolutions to be introduced at the meeting shall be filed at the 
Office of the Town Clerk at least 24 hours in advance of said meeting. 
 
For the avoidance of doubt, any Resolution filed by a Member of the Town Board prior to 
a Regular Meeting in accordan ce with the Rules herein shall be called during “Call of & 
Action Upon Resolutions” irrespective of any guidelines established for or in connection 
with the use of Agenda Management software and any Resolutions filed subsequent to the 
reading of Resolution s at the Work Session preceding the Town Board meeting shall be 
added to the Final Agenda and shall be scheduled to be called sequentially in the order in 
which such Resolution/s are filed AND following consideration of those Resolutions that 
were read during the Work Session preceding the Town Board meeting.   Generally, such 
Resolutions should follow the usual and customary Resolution titled, “Pays Bills”. 
 
 RESOLUTIONS FROM THE FLOOR 
 
Resolutions “from the floor” shall be those resolutions that were not f iled in the Office of 
Town Clerk in accordance with the rules set forth above.  Resolutions “from the floor” 
shall be offered only after all other Resolutions properly appearing on the Final Agenda 
have been acted upon and the proponent or sponsor of such, who shall be a Member of the 
Town Board, has requested and been granted the floor.   Such Resolutions should be rare 
and offered due to articulable exigent circumstance. 
 
In order to call a Resolution “from the floor” copies of the proposed Resolution shall have 
been provided to all Members of the Town Board, the Office of the Town Supervisor, the 
Town Board Coordinator, the Town Attorney and the Town Clerk at least thirty (30) 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 159
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-11- 
minutes prior to the start of the Meeting and additional copies shall be availa ble for 
members of the audience and any news outlet attending the meeting.   
 
Calling a Resolution “from the floor” shall require the attendance of at least four (4) Town 
Board Members and the affirmative vote of three (3) Members of the Town Board present 
at the Meeting.  The proponent of the Resolution shall have the opportunity to explain the 
Resolution and the need and urgency therefor but there shall be no debate on the action. If 
such Resolution shall achieve three (3) affirmative votes, the Resolution shall be thereafter 
subject to comment from the public, moved, seconded, debated and acted upon in the 
normal course. 
 
This Rule XIV may only be suspended by affirmative, unanimous vote of all Members of the Town 
Board. 
 
 
RULE XV. OTHER ADDITIONS TO THE AGENDA 
 
New items may be added to the Agenda during any Regular or Special Town Board 
Meeting upon the affirmative vote of any three (3) members of the Town Board and such 
new items shall be designated as “Items Proposed for Con sideration upon Special 
Consent.” Items under this Rule shall not be resolutions which are addressed specifically 
hereinabove. 
 
 
RULE XVI. CONSTITUTION OF STANDING COMMITTEES 
 
The following standing committees consisting of three members shall be appointed by the 
Supervisor at the Organizational Meeting of the Town Board or as soon thereafter as may 
be practical. 
  
1. Community Development Agency Finance Committee; and  
2. The Community Development Agency Audit Committee. 
The first named member of each committee shall be Chairman.  The Supervisor shall be a 
non-voting ex officio member of every committee. 
 
Two members shall constitute a quorum.  Where practical, reports of committees should 
be in writing and signed by at least two members. 
 
Standing Committees shall meet at the call of their Chairman or any of the three members. 
 
The Chairman of each Standing Committee shall have delivered to Committee members a 
two day notice, in writing, stating the time, the place and the purpose of the Committee 
meeting.  Every Town Board member has the right to attend any Standing Committee 
meeting called whether a designated member of that Standing Committee or not. 
 
 
9.21.a
Packet Pg. 160
Attachment: Amended Rules of the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead_FINAL  (2025-230 : Amends Adopted Rules and Procedures for Town
Rev. February 18, 2025 
 
-12- 
 
RULE XVII. YEAR END REMOVAL OF ITEMS 
 
Any proposed local law, resolution or other item other than la nd use applications tabled 
and pending as of December 31 of any given year shall be automatically removed on such 
date unless such item was tabled at the final Meeting of the Town Board of the current 
year. 
  
 
RULE XVIII. AMENDMENT, MODIFICATION OR REPEAL OF RULES 
 
Permanent amendment, modification or repeal of the rules in whole or in part may be made 
at any time by a Resolution of the Town Board at a regular or special meeting.
